20. Valid Parentheses ^358ejAda

Hint ^szRn0VDG

Given a string s containing just the characters '(', ')', '{', '}', '[' and ']', determine if the input string is valid. ^TuVDqzBx

An input string is valid if: ^cC07GADq

Open brackets must be closed by the same type of brackets. ^gYekLu2t

Open brackets must be closed in the correct order. ^tkv5ptii

Every close bracket has a corresponding open bracket of the same type. ^lQRnEnHT

Example 1: ^poYoj309

Input: s = "()" ^u6UwTIUX

Output: true ^EDkbCUQG

Example 2: ^2eoRjgBy

Input: s = "()[]{}" ^Q0UDIo2T

Output: true ^lTVwYs86

Example 3: ^fZc8hkAN

Input: s = "(]" ^paq95jNt

Output: false ^zViQ7Fqs

Example 4: ^4GBo1BhP

Input: s = "([])" ^OHNjUJUM

Output: true ^zvKcMNzW

[1,8,6,2,5,4,8,3,7] ^oeUf24Ue

[2,3,4] ^1DNJkI6X

[2,7,11,15] ^BZRrdw96

[-1,0] ^eJFRbs1b
